<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">pièce</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pettia</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gaulish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gaulish language">Gaulish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cel-gau">*pettyā‎</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Celtic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Celtic language">Proto-Celtic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="cel-pro">*kʷezdis</i>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пьяненький.html>пья́ненький</a> (20624)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***пьянеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пьянеть.html>пьяне́ть</a> (19713)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пьянеть.html>пьяне́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pʹjanétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:опьянеть.html>опьяне́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to get intoxicated/tipsy/inebriated</li>
<li>to get intoxicated <i>(with joy, success etc)</i></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пьяный.html>пья́но</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pʹjáno</span>)

***пьяный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пьяный.html>пья́ный</a> (8440)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">пиꙗнъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pijanŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pijanъ</i>, passive participle of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pijati</i>, iterative aspect of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*piti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to drink</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пьяный.html>пья́ный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pʹjányj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)пьяне́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:пьянеть.html>пьяне́й</a></b>)

<ol><li>drunk</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***пядь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пядь.html>пядь</a> (23542)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:пядь.html>пядь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pjadĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pędь</i>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">п'ядь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pʺjadʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">пѧдь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pędĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">píď</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovak_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovak language">Slovak</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sk">piaď</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">piędź</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Upper_Sorbian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Upper Sorbian language">Upper Sorbian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="hsb">pjedź</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lower_Sorbian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lower Sorbian language">Lower Sorbian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dsb">pěź</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sh">pȇd</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovene_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovene language">Slovene</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">ре̣̑d</i>. Related to <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пнуть.html>пнуть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пядь.html>пядь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pjadʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пядь.html>пя́ди</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пядь.html>пя́ди</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пядь.html>пяде́й</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пядь.html>пя́дей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> span <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">Old Russian unit of length corresponding to the distance between the spaced ends of the thumb and index fingers, seven inches, 17.78 cm</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> small area of land</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> hand</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> sole of the foot, foot</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пялиться.html>пя́лившийся</a> (13851)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пялиться.html>пя́лившийся</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pjálivšijsja</span>)

***пялить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пялить.html>пя́лить</a> (22984)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пя́ло</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pjálo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-itʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pędlo</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">embroidery hoop</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пялить.html>пя́лить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pjálitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to stretch tight, to put on (clothing) with difficulty</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">idiomatic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span>:
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пялить.html>пя́лить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:глаз.html>глаза́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> кого́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pjálitʹ</b> glazá na kovó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to stare at someone</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***пялиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пялиться.html>пя́литься</a> (13851)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пялиться.html>пя́литься</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pjálitʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to stare, to gaze</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>пя́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ться</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4a.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-пял-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***пята.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пята.html>пята́</a> (10334)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pęta</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg"><a href = vnd.unilang:петый.html>пе́та</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">peta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovene_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovene language">Slovene</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">peta</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sh">peta</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovak_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovak language">Slovak</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sk">päta</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пята.html>пята́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pjatá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пята.html>пяты́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пята.html>пяты́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пята.html>пят</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> heel; foot
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>головы́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пята.html>пят</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s golový do <b>pjat</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">from head to <b>toe</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>wide foot of a support, mainstay, pier, or buttress</li></ol>

***пятак.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пятак.html>пята́к</a> (9936)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пятак.html>пята́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pjaták</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пятак.html>пятака́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пятак.html>пятаки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пятак.html>пятако́в</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пятачок.html>пятачо́к</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>five-kopeck coin</li>
<li>five roubles, five dollars, etc.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> muzzle, mug (face); schnozzle, conk, honker, schnoz, snoot (nose)</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пятак.html>пята́к</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pjaták</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́к</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пятачок.html>пятачо́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pjatačók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пятачок.html>пятачка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пятачок.html>пятачки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пятачок.html>пятачко́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Diminutive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пятак.html>пята́к</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pjaták</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>: five-kopeck coin <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">out of use</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> pig's snout</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a small patch of land</li></ol>

***пятеро.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пятеро.html>пя́теро</a> (4864)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Numeral">Numeral</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пятеро.html>пя́теро</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pjátero</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>five (in a group together), fivesome, five of them
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пятеро.html>пя́теро</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>дете́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pjátero</b> detéj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">five children</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пятеро.html>пя́теро</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>часо́в</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pjátero</b> časóv</i> ― <span class="e-translation">five watches</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пятеро.html>пя́теро</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>очко́в</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pjátero</b> očkóv</i> ― <span class="e-translation">five pairs of glasses</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пятеро.html>пя́теро</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>нас</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pjátero</b> iz nas</i> ― <span class="e-translation">five of us</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>нас</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ло</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пятеро.html>пя́теро</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nas býlo <b>pjátero</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">there were five of us</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The nominative of a collective numeral governs the genitive plural of the noun, pronoun, or adjective. The other cases agree with that of the noun, pronoun, or adjective. Not used with feminine nouns. Used mostly when speaking of children and with a few nouns that are used in the plural only, such as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>часы́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">časý</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>очки́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">očkí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, or with pronouns.
</p>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>пя́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>те</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ро</b>
</p><p>Числительное, <a href = vnd.unilang:собирательный.html>собира́тельное</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:употребляться.html>Употребля́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>существи́тельными</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́го</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>или</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:общий.html>о́бщего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>рода</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:обозначающий.html>обознача́ющими</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>ли́ц</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>существи́тельными</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:имеющий.html>име́ющими</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:только.html>то́лько</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:множественный.html>мно́жественное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:число.html>число</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:личный.html>ли́чными</a> местоимениями <a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:множественный.html>мно́жественном</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:число.html>числе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:без.html>без</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:зависимый.html>зави́симого</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>слова</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-пят-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ер</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-о</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пять.html>пять</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pjatʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">five</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>лет</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">let</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">year</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пятилетка.html>пятиле́тка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pjatilétka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пятилетка.html>пятиле́тки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пятилетка.html>пятиле́тки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пятилетка.html>пятиле́ток</a></b>)

***пятнадцать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пятнадцать.html>пятна́дцать</a> (1435)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compounded from <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пять.html>пять</a></b> + <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> + <b>дцать</b>, or <i>five on ten</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Numeral">Numeral</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пятнадцать.html>пятна́дцать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pjatnádcatʹ</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>fifteen (15)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:пятнадцать.html>пятна́дцать</a></strong></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pjatnadcatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> in the nominative case and accusative case governs the genitive plural of the noun. In other cases, it governs the corresponding plural case of the noun.
</p>
<ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пятнадцать.html>пятна́дцать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчиков</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pjatnádcatʹ</b> málʹčikov</i> ― <span class="e-translation">fifteen boys</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пятнадцать.html>пятна́дцатью</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчиками</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s <b>pjatnádcatʹju</b> málʹčikami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">with fifteen boys</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчиков</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пятнадцать.html>пятна́дцать</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">málʹčikov <b>pjatnádcatʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">approximately fifteen boys</span></div></li></ul>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пята.html>пят</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:над.html>на́д</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>цать</b>
</p><p>Числительное, <a href = vnd.unilang:количественный.html>коли́чественное</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующее</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:порядковый.html>поря́дковое</a> числительное — <a href = vnd.unilang:пятнадцатый.html>пятна́дцатый</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-пят-</b>; суффикс: <b>-надцать</b>.
</p>

***пятница.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пятница.html>пя́тница</a> (4854)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пять.html>пять</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pjatʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">five</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ница</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nica</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, since Friday is the fifth day of the week (counting from Monday). Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">пя́тниця</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pjátnycja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, Old East Slavic пятъкъ, Old Church Slavonic <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">пѧтъкъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pętŭkŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, Bulgarian <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg">пе́тък</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pétǎk</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg">пе́тка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pétka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, and Serbo-Croatian <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">пе́так</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пятница.html>пя́тница</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pjátnica</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пятница.html>пя́тницы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пятница.html>пя́тницы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пятница.html>пя́тниц</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Friday
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пятница.html>пя́тницу</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>pjátnicu</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">on <b>Friday</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пятница.html>пя́тницам</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">po <b>pjátnicam</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">on <b>Fridays</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пятница.html>пя́тнице</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">k <b>pjátnice</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">by <b>Friday</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пятница.html>пя́тницы</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s <b>pjátnicy</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">from <b>Friday</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пятница.html>пя́тницы</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пятница.html>пя́тницы</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s <b>pjátnicy</b> do <b>pjátnicy</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">from <b>Friday</b> to <b>Friday</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:следующий.html>сле́дующую</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пятница.html>пя́тницу</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v slédujuščuju <b>pjátnicu</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">next <b>Friday</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:семь.html>семь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пятница.html>пя́тниц</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:неделя.html>неде́ле</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u nevó semʹ pjátnic na nedéle</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he keeps changing his mind</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">he's got seven Fridays in a week</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пята.html>пя́т</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ца</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 5a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-пят-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ниц</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***пять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пять.html>пять</a> (281)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">пѧть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pętĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pętь</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*pénkʷe</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">five</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">fünf</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">cinque</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">cinq</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Greek_language" class="extiw" title="w:Greek language">Greek</a></span> <i class="Grek mention" lang="el">πέντε</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="el-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pénte</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">پَنج</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="fa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pænj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">पञ्च</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pañca</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Numeral">Numeral</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пять.html>пять</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pjatʹ</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>five (5)</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:пять.html>пять</a></strong></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pjatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> in the nominative case and accusative case governs the genitive plural of the noun. In other cases, it governs the corresponding plural case of the noun.
</p>
<ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пять.html>пять</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчиков</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pjatʹ</b> málʹčikov</i> ― <span class="e-translation">five boys</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пять.html>пятью́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчиками</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s <b>pjatʹjú</b> málʹčikami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">with five boys</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчиков</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пять.html>пять</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">málʹčikov <b>pjatʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">approximately five boys</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пятьдесят.html>пятьдеся́т</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пять.html>пять</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́г</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pjatʹdesját <b>pjatʹ</b> knig</i> ― <span class="e-translation">fifty-five books</span></div></li></ul>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пять.html>пять</a></b>
</p><p>Числительное, <a href = vnd.unilang:количественный.html>коли́чественное</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующее</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:порядковый.html>поря́дковое</a> числительное — <a href = vnd.unilang:пятый.html>пя́тый</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>Встреча́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:написание.html>написа́ния</a>: 5, V.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-пять-</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>
